function SpamBaller()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value =3D=3D "Baller" and gam=
e.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
while _G.BallerFarm do
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer()
wait(30.05)
end
end
end

function SpamReplica()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value =3D=3D "Replica" and ga=
me.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.IsInDefaultArena.Value =3D=3D true then
while ReplicaFarm do
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Duplicate:FireServer(true)
wait(20)
end
end
end

function SpamBlink()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value =3D=3D "Blink" and game=
.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then

 =3D Vector3.new(0, 0, 0),["ismoving"] =3D false,["mousebehavior"] =3D Enum=
.MouseBehavior.Default})

end
end
end

hen

racter,false)

afeBox"].CFrame * CFrame.new(0,5,0)

PotionThrowNukeAuto =3D Tab14:AddToggle({
	Name =3D "Auto Throw Nuke Potion",
	Default =3D false,
	Callback =3D function(Value)
_G.AutoThrowPotion =3D Value
if _G.AutoThrowPotion =3D=3D false then
if game.Workspace.CurrentCamera and game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.=
Character and game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChi=
ldOfClass("Humanoid") then
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject =3D game:GetService("Players").L=
ocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
end
end
if _G.AutoThrowPotion =3D=3D true and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:Fi=
ndFirstChild("entered") =3D=3D nil and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats=
.Glove.Value =3D=3D "Alchemist" then
if _G.AutoThrowPotion =3D=3D true then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D game.workspa=
ce.Origo.CFrame
if _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Arena" then
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject =3D game.workspace.Origo
elseif _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Island Slapple" then
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject =3D game.workspace.Arena.island5=
.Union
elseif _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Tournament" then
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject =3D workspace.Battlearena.Arena
elseif _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Moai Island" then
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject =3D game.Workspace.Arena.island4=
.Grass
elseif _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Player" then=20
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject =3D game.workspace.Origo
end
elseif _G.AutoThrowPotion =3D=3D false then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D game.workspa=
ce.Origo.CFrame
end
while _G.AutoThrowPotion do
local RandomTeleX =3D math.random(-_G.NukeExtend,_G.NukeExtend)
local RandomTeleZ =3D math.random(-_G.NukeExtend,_G.NukeExtend)
if _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Arena" then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D game.workspa=
ce.Origo.CFrame * CFrame.new(RandomTeleX,_G.NukeHeightPotion,RandomTeleZ)
elseif _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Island Slapple" then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D game.workspa=
ce.Arena.island5.Union.CFrame * CFrame.new(RandomTeleX,_G.NukeHeightPotion,=
RandomTeleZ)
elseif _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Tournament" then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D workspace.Ba=
ttlearena.Arena.CFrame * CFrame.new(RandomTeleX,_G.NukeHeightPotion,RandomT=
eleZ)
elseif _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Moai Island" then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D game.Workspa=
ce.Arena.island4.Grass.CFrame * CFrame.new(RandomTeleX,_G.NukeHeightPotion,=
RandomTeleZ)
elseif _G.PhaceNuke =3D=3D "Player" then
local players =3D game.Players:GetChildren()
local randomPlayer =3D players[math.random(1, #players)]
repeat randomPlayer =3D players[math.random(1, #players)] until randomPlaye=
r ~=3D game.Players.LocalPlayer and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("=
entered") and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("ded") =3D=3D nil and r=
andomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("InLabyrinth") =3D=3D nil and randomPl=
ayer.Character:FindFirstChild("rock") =3D=3D nil
Target =3D randomPlayer
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D Target.Chara=
cter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,_G.NukeHeightPotion,5)
end
task.wait()
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").AlchemistEvent:FireServer("UsePotion",=
_G.PotionThrownNuke,true)
end
elseif _G.AutoThrowPotion =3D=3D true then
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name =3D "Error",Content =3D "You dont't have Al=
chemist equipped, or you have in the lobby",Image =3D "rbxassetid://7733658=
504",Time =3D 5})
wait(0.05)
PotionThrowNukeAuto:Set(false)
end
	end   =20
})

PingPong =3D Tab14:AddToggle({
	Name =3D "Ping Pong Orbit",
	Default =3D false,
	Callback =3D function(Value)
		PingPongOrbit =3D Value
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value =3D=3D "Ping Pong" then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.RadioPart.Rotation =3D game.Player=
s.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Rotation
Orbit =3D "0"
if OrbitSpeed =3D=3D nil then
OrbitSpeed =3D 1
end
PingPongBall =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name.."_PingPongBall"
while PingPongOrbit and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value =
=3D=3D "Ping Pong" do
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer()
Orbit =3D Orbit + OrbitSpeed
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.RadioPart.Rotation =3D Vector3.new=
(-180, Orbit, -180)
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.RadioPart:GetChildren()[2] then
for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.ClassName =3D=3D "Part" and v.Name =3D=3D PingPong=
Ball then
v.CFrame =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.RadioPart.CFrame * CF=
rame.new(0,0,-_G.ExtendPingPong) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0), math.rad(-90)=
, math.rad(0))
                    end
                end
for i,v in pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.RadioPart:GetChil=
dren()) do
                    if v.ClassName =3D=3D "Part" and v.Name =3D=3D PingPong=
Ball then
                        v.CFrame =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Tor=
so.RadioPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,_G.ExtendPingPong) * CFrame.Angles(mat=
h.rad(0), math.rad(90), math.rad(0))
                    end
                end
elseif game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.RadioPart:GetChildren()[1] =
or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.RadioPart:GetChildren()[2] then
for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.ClassName =3D=3D "Part" and v.Name =3D=3D PingPong=
Ball then
v.Parent =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.RadioPart
break
                    end
                end
end
task.wait(0.01)
end
elseif Value =3D=3D true then
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name =3D "Error",Content =3D "You don't have Pin=
g Pong equipped.",Image =3D "rbxassetid://7733658504",Time =3D 5})
wait(0.05)
PingPong:Set(false)
end
	end   =20
})

tion:lower() then

,Image =3D "rbxassetid://7733658504",Time =3D 5})

ReplicaAndReverse =3D Tab14:AddToggle({

		ReplicaAndReverseGet =3D Value=20
if _G.GetSlapGot =3D=3D "Normal" then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") =3D=3D nil =
and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value =3D=3D "Reverse" then

coroutine.wrap(SpamReplicaReverse)()=20
end

if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and game.Pl=
ayers.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health ~=3D 0 then

                 if v.Name:match(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name) and v:FindF=
irstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").b:FireServer(v:WaitForChild("Head"),tr=
ue)
end
                 end
end
task.wait()
end
elseif ReplicaAndReverseGet =3D=3D true then=20
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name =3D "Error",Content =3D "You don't have Rev=
erse equipped or you have in lobby.",Image =3D "rbxassetid://7733658504",Ti=
me =3D 5})=20
wait(0.05)
ReplicaAndReverse:Set(false)=20
end
elseif _G.GetSlapGot =3D=3D "Fast =C3=97 Slap Farm [ Lag ]" then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") =3D=3D nil =
and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value =3D=3D "Reverse" then
if ReplicaAndReverseGet =3D=3D true then=20
coroutine.wrap(SpamReplicaReverse)()=20
end
while ReplicaAndReverseGet do=20
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and game.Pl=
ayers.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health ~=3D 0 then
for i, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do=20
                 if v.Name:match(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name) and v:FindF=
irstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
for i =3D 1,_G.SlapFarmGet do
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and game.Pl=
ayers.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health ~=3D 0 then
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").b:FireServer(v:WaitForChild("Head"),tr=
ue)
end
end
end
                 end
end
task.wait(0.07)
end
elseif ReplicaAndReverseGet =3D=3D true then=20

	end   =20

Tab7:AddToggle({
	Name =3D "Start Fly",
	Default =3D false,
	Callback =3D function(Value)
	 _G.StartFly =3D Value
if _G.StartFly =3D=3D false then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Characte=
r:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.=
Humanoid.RootPart and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart:F=
indFirstChild("VelocityHandler") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Hum=
anoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler:Destroy=
()
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler:Destroy()
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand =3D false
end
end
while _G.StartFly do
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Characte=
r:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.=
Humanoid.RootPart and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart:F=
indFirstChild("VelocityHandler") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Hum=
anoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.MaxForc=
e =3D Vector3.new(9e9,9e9,9e9)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler.MaxTorque =
=3D Vector3.new(9e9,9e9,9e9)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand =3D true
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler.CFrame =3D =
Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D Vector3.new()
if require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModul=
e"):WaitForChild("ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().X &gt; 0 then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.V=
elocity + game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.RightVector * (require(game.P=
layers.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModule"):WaitForChild(=
"ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().X * _G.SetSpeedFly)
end
if require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModul=
e"):WaitForChild("ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().X &lt; 0 then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.V=
elocity + game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.RightVector * (require(game.P=
layers.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModule"):WaitForChild(=
"ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().X * _G.SetSpeedFly)
end
if require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModul=
e"):WaitForChild("ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().Z &gt; 0 then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.V=
elocity - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.LookVector * (require(game.Pl=
ayers.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModule"):WaitForChild("=
ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().Z * _G.SetSpeedFly)
end
if require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModul=
e"):WaitForChild("ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().Z &lt; 0 then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.V=
elocity - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.LookVector * (require(game.Pl=
ayers.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModule"):WaitForChild("=
ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().Z * _G.SetSpeedFly)
end
elseif game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Char=
acter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Charac=
ter.Humanoid.RootPart and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPa=
rt:FindFirstChild("VelocityHandler") =3D=3D nil and game.Players.LocalPlaye=
r.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler") =3D=3D nil then
local bv =3D Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
local bg =3D Instance.new("BodyGyro")

bv.Name =3D "VelocityHandler"
bv.Parent =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
bv.MaxForce =3D Vector3.new(0,0,0)
bv.Velocity =3D Vector3.new(0,0,0)

bg.Name =3D "GyroHandler"
bg.Parent =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
bg.MaxTorque =3D Vector3.new(0,0,0)
bg.P =3D 1000
bg.D =3D 50
end
task.wait()
end
	end   =20
})

while _G.AutoFarmSlap do
for i,v in pairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
if v ~=3D game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:F=
indFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v.Character then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and v.Chara=
cter:FindFirstChild("entered") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRoot=
Part") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("stevebody") =3D=3D nil and v.Charact=
er:FindFirstChild("rock") =3D=3D nil and v.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Brick=
Color ~=3D BrickColor.new("New Yeller") and v.Character.Ragdolled.Value =3D=
=3D false then
if v.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("UnoReverseCard") =3D=3D nil or game.Pla=
yers.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value =3D=3D "Error" then
if _G.AutoFarmSlap =3D=3D true then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D v.Character:=
FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame * CFrame.new(0,_G.HipAutoFarmSlap=
,0)
task.wait(0.5)
gloveHits[game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value]:FireServer(v.Ch=
aracter:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart"),true)
task.wait(0.43)
end
end
end
end
end
task.wait()
end
	end   =20
})

Tab7:AddButton({
	Name =3D "Serverhop",
	Callback =3D function()
local serverList =3D {}
for _, v in ipairs(game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(game:HttpGetAs=
ync("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. game.PlaceId .. "/servers/Publi=
c?sortOrder=3DAsc&amp;limit=3D100")).data) do
	if v.playing and type(v) =3D=3D "table" and v.maxPlayers &gt; v.playing an=
d v.id ~=3D game.JobId then
		serverList[#serverList + 1] =3D v.id
	end
end
if #serverList &gt; 0 then
	game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, s=
erverList[math.random(1, #serverList)])
end
	end
})

	Callback =3D function(Value)
_G.Transparency =3D Value

game.Workspace["VoidPart"]["TAntiVoid"].Transparency =3D Value
elseif _G.AntiVoidChoose =3D=3D "Retro" then
game.Workspace["Psycho"]["Retro1"].Transparency =3D Value
game.Workspace["Psycho"]["Retro1"]["Retro2"].Transparency =3D Value
game.Workspace["Psycho"]["Retro1"]["Retro3"].Transparency =3D Value
elseif _G.AntiVoidChoose =3D=3D "Water" then
game.Workspace["Psycho"]["Kraken"].Transparency =3D Value
elseif _G.AntiVoidChoose =3D=3D "Psycho" then
game.Workspace["Psycho"].Transparency =3D Value
elseif _G.AntiVoidChoose =3D=3D "Bob" then
game.Workspace["VoidPart"]["TAntiVoid"].Transparency =3D Value
game.Workspace["BobWalk1"].Transparency =3D Value
for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace.BobWalk1:GetChildren()) do
v.Transparency =3D _G.Transparency
end
end
end
	end   =20
})

AntiRecord =3D Tab2:AddToggle({
	Name =3D "Anti Record",
	Default =3D false,
	Callback =3D function(Value)
_G.AntiRecord =3D Value
	end   =20
})
for i,p in pairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
if p ~=3D game.Players.LocalPlayer then
p.Chatted:Connect(function(message)
Words =3D message:split(" ")
if _G.AntiRecord =3D=3D true then
for i, v in pairs(Words) do
if v:lower():match("recording") or v:lower():match(" rec") or v:lower():mat=
ch("record") or v:lower():match("discor") or v:lower():match(" disco") or v=
:lower():match(" disc") or v:lower():match("ticket") or v:lower():match("ti=
ckets") or v:lower():match(" ds") or v:lower():match(" dc") or v:lower():ma=
tch("dizzy") or v:lower():match("dizzycord") or v:lower():match(" clip") or=
 v:lower():match("proof") or v:lower():match("evidence") then
AntiKick:Set(false)
game.Players.LocalPlayer:Kick("Possible player recording detected.".." [ ".=
.p.Name.." ]".." [ "..message.." ]")
end
end
end
end)
end
end
game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(Player)
Player.Chatted:Connect(function(message)
Words =3D message:split(" ")
if _G.AntiRecord =3D=3D true then
for i, v in pairs(Words) do
if v:lower():match("recording") or v:lower():match(" rec") or v:lower():mat=
ch("record") or v:lower():match("discor") or v:lower():match(" disco") or v=
:lower():match(" disc") or v:lower():match("ticket") or v:lower():match("ti=
ckets") or v:lower():match(" ds") or v:lower():match(" dc") or v:lower():ma=
tch("dizzy") or v:lower():match("dizzycord") or v:lower():match(" clip") or=
 v:lower():match("proof") or v:lower():match("evidence") then
AntiKick:Set(false)
game.Players.LocalPlayer:Kick("Possible player recording detected.".." [ ".=
.Player.Name.." ]".." [ "..message.." ]")
end
end
end
end)
end)

Tab3:AddButton({
	Name =3D "Get Counter + Elude",
	Callback =3D function()
if _G.SelectMaze =3D=3D "Teleport" then
local teleportFunc =3D queueonteleport or queue_on_teleport
if teleportFunc then
    teleportFunc([[
        if not game:IsLoaded() then
            game.Loaded:Wait()
        end
        repeat wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer
        wait(3)
Time =3D 121
fireclickdetector(game.Workspace.CounterLever.ClickDetector)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D CFrame.new(0=
,100,0)
wait(0.2)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored =3D true
for i =3D 1,Time do
Time =3D Time - 1
game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{Title =3D "Error"=
,Text =3D "You wait time [ "..Time.." ] receive.",Icon =3D "rbxassetid://77=
33658504",Duration =3D 1})
wait(1)
end
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored =3D false
wait(0.5)
firetouchinterest(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirs=
tChild("HumanoidRootPart"), game.Workspace.Ruins.Elude.Glove, 0)
firetouchinterest(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirs=
tChild("HumanoidRootPart"), game.Workspace.Ruins.Elude.Glove, 1)
for i,v in pairs(workspace.Maze:GetDescendants()) do
if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
fireclickdetector(v)
end
end
    ]])
end
game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(11828384869)
elseif _G.SelectMaze =3D=3D "Auto Keypad" then
if not workspace:FindFirstChild("Keypad") then
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name =3D "Error",Content =3D "Server don't have =
keypad, auto start Serverhop",Image =3D "rbxassetid://7733658504",Time =3D =
5})
	for _, server in ipairs(game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGetAsync("htt=
ps://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. game.PlaceId .. "/servers/Public?sortOr=
der=3DAsc&amp;limit=3D100")).data) do
    	if server.playing &lt; server.maxPlayers and server.JobId ~=3D game.Jo=
bId then
        	game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.Pl=
aceId, server.id)
    	end
	end
else
local teleportFunc =3D queueonteleport or queue_on_teleport
if teleportFunc then
    teleportFunc([[
        if not game:IsLoaded() then
            game.Loaded:Wait()
        end
        repeat wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer
        wait(3)
Time =3D 121
fireclickdetector(game.Workspace.CounterLever.ClickDetector)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =3D CFrame.new(0=
,100,0)
wait(0.2)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored =3D true
for i =3D 1,Time do
Time =3D Time - 1
game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{Title =3D "Error"=
,Text =3D "You wait time [ "..Time.." ] receive.",Icon =3D "rbxassetid://77=
33658504",Duration =3D 1})
wait(1)
end
firetouchinterest(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirs=
tChild("HumanoidRootPart"), game.Workspace.Ruins.Elude.Glove, 0)
firetouchinterest(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirs=
tChild("HumanoidRootPart"), game.Workspace.Ruins.Elude.Glove, 1)
for i,v in pairs(workspace.Maze:GetDescendants()) do
if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
fireclickdetector(v)
end
end
    ]])
end
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name =3D "Error",Content =3D "Server in have spa=
wn keypad, auto start keypad",Image =3D "rbxassetid://7733658504",Time =3D =
5})
game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject =3D workspace.Keypad.Buttons.Ent=
er
fireclickdetector(workspace:WaitForChild("Keypad").Buttons:FindFirstChild("=
Reset").ClickDetector)
local digits =3D tostring((#game.Players:GetPlayers()) * 25 + 1100 - 7)
for i =3D 1, #digits do
task.wait(0.8)
local digit =3D digits:sub(i, i)
fireclickdetector(workspace:WaitForChild("Keypad").Buttons:FindFirstChild(d=
igit).ClickDetector)
end
task.wait(0.5)
fireclickdetector(workspace:WaitForChild("Keypad").Buttons:FindFirstChild("=
Enter").ClickDetector)
end
end
  	end   =20
})

=3D 5})

Tab5:AddToggle({
	Name =3D "Walkspeed Set Auto",
	Default =3D false,
	Callback =3D function(Value)
		KeepWalkspeed =3D Value
            while KeepWalkspeed do
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Human=
oid") ~=3D nil and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed ~=
=3D Walkspeed then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed =
=3D Walkspeed
                end
task.wait()
            end
	end   =20
})

     end)

_G.SetSpeedFly =3D 100
Tab:AddToggle({
	Name =3D "Start Fly",
	Default =3D false,
	Callback =3D function(Value)
	 _G.StartFly =3D Value
if _G.StartFly =3D=3D false then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Characte=
r:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.=
Humanoid.RootPart and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart:F=
indFirstChild("VelocityHandler") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Hum=
anoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler:Destroy=
()
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler:Destroy()
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand =3D false
end
end
while _G.StartFly do
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Characte=
r:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.=
Humanoid.RootPart and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart:F=
indFirstChild("VelocityHandler") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Hum=
anoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.MaxForc=
e =3D Vector3.new(9e9,9e9,9e9)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler.MaxTorque =
=3D Vector3.new(9e9,9e9,9e9)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand =3D true
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler.CFrame =3D =
Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D Vector3.new()
if require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModul=
e"):WaitForChild("ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().X &gt; 0 then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.V=
elocity + game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.RightVector * (require(game.P=
layers.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModule"):WaitForChild(=
"ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().X * _G.SetSpeedFly)
end
if require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModul=
e"):WaitForChild("ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().X &lt; 0 then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.V=
elocity + game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.RightVector * (require(game.P=
layers.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModule"):WaitForChild(=
"ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().X * _G.SetSpeedFly)
end
if require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModul=
e"):WaitForChild("ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().Z &gt; 0 then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.V=
elocity - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.LookVector * (require(game.Pl=
ayers.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModule"):WaitForChild("=
ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().Z * _G.SetSpeedFly)
end
if require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModul=
e"):WaitForChild("ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().Z &lt; 0 then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocit=
y =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.V=
elocity - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.LookVector * (require(game.Pl=
ayers.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("PlayerModule"):WaitForChild("=
ControlModule")):GetMoveVector().Z * _G.SetSpeedFly)
end
elseif game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Char=
acter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Charac=
ter.Humanoid.RootPart and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPa=
rt:FindFirstChild("VelocityHandler") =3D=3D nil and game.Players.LocalPlaye=
r.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler") =3D=3D nil then
local bv =3D Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
local bg =3D Instance.new("BodyGyro")

bv.Name =3D "VelocityHandler"
bv.Parent =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
bv.MaxForce =3D Vector3.new(0,0,0)
bv.Velocity =3D Vector3.new(0,0,0)

bg.Name =3D "GyroHandler"
bg.Parent =3D game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
bg.MaxTorque =3D Vector3.new(0,0,0)
bg.P =3D 1000
bg.D =3D 50
end
task.wait()
end
	end   =20
})

); L:Stop(); Laugh:Stop(); Parker:Stop(); Spasm:Stop(); Thriller:Stop()
end
end
end)
    end   =20

Tab1:AddDropdown({
	Name =3D "Remove",
	Default =3D "",
	Options =3D {"Lava", "Zone Blur", "Acid"},
	Callback =3D function(Value)
if Value =3D=3D "Lava" then
for _, v in ipairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):GetDescendants()) do
    if v.Name =3D=3D "Lava" then
        v:Destroy()
    end
end
elseif Value =3D=3D "Zone Blur" then
for _, v in ipairs(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):GetDescendants()) d=
o
    if v.Name =3D=3D "ZoneEffects" then
        v:Destroy()
    end
end
elseif Value =3D=3D "Acid" then
for _, v in ipairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):GetDescendants()) do
    if v.Name =3D=3D "Acid" then
        v:Destroy()
    end
end
end
	end   =20
})

Tab1:AddDropdown({
	Name =3D "Safe",
	Default =3D "",
	Options =3D {"Lava", "Zone Blur Remove", "Acid"},
	Callback =3D function(Value)
if Value =3D=3D "Lava" then
workspace.Map.DragonDepths.Lava.CanTouch =3D false
elseif Value =3D=3D "Zone Blur Remove" then
for _, v in ipairs(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):GetDescendants()) d=
o
    if v.Name =3D=3D "ZoneEffects" then
        v:Destroy()
    end
end
elseif Value =3D=3D "Acid" then
for _,v in ipairs(workspace.Map.AcidAbnormality:GetChildren()) do
			if v.Name =3D=3D "Acid" and v:IsA("BasePart") and v:FindFirstChildWhichI=
sA("TouchTransmitter") then
				v.CanTouch =3D false
			end
		end
end
	end   =20
})

Tab1:AddToggle({
	Name =3D "Anti Record",
	Default =3D false,
	Callback =3D function(Value)
AntiRecord =3D Value
	end   =20
})
for i,p in pairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
if p ~=3D game.Players.LocalPlayer then
p.Chatted:Connect(function(message)
Words =3D message:split(" ")
if AntiRecord =3D=3D true then
for i, v in pairs(Words) do
if v:lower():match("recording") or v:lower():match(" rec") or v:lower():mat=
ch("record") or v:lower():match("discor") or v:lower():match(" disco") or v=
:lower():match(" disc") or v:lower():match("ticket") or v:lower():match("ti=
ckets") or v:lower():match(" ds") or v:lower():match(" dc") or v:lower():ma=
tch("dizzy") or v:lower():match("dizzycord") or v:lower():match(" clip") or=
 v:lower():match("proof") or v:lower():match("evidence") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer:Kick("Possible player recording detected.".." [ ".=
.p.Name.." ]".." [ "..message.." ]")
end
end
end
end)
end
end
game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(Player)
Player.Chatted:Connect(function(message)
Words =3D message:split(" ")
if AntiRecord =3D=3D true then
for i, v in pairs(Words) do
if v:lower():match("recording") or v:lower():match(" rec") or v:lower():mat=
ch("record") or v:lower():match("discor") or v:lower():match(" disco") or v=
:lower():match(" disc") or v:lower():match("ticket") or v:lower():match("ti=
ckets") or v:lower():match(" ds") or v:lower():match(" dc") or v:lower():ma=
tch("dizzy") or v:lower():match("dizzycord") or v:lower():match(" clip") or=
 v:lower():match("proof") or v:lower():match("evidence") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer:Kick("Possible player recording detected.".." [ ".=
.Player.Name.." ]".." [ "..message.." ]")
end
end
end
end)
end)

Tab1:AddToggle({
	Name =3D "Anti Ragdoll",
	Default =3D false,
	Callback =3D function(Value)
        _G.AntiRagdoll =3D Value
while _G.AntiRagdoll  do
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Characte=
r:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value =3D=
=3D true then
repeat task.wait() game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored =3D tr=
ue
until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value =
=3D=3D false
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored =3D false
end
end
task.wait()
end
	end   =20
})
